    SELECT `e0`.`Id`, `e0`.`CompanyId`, `e0`.`CreatedAt`, `e0`.`DeletedAt`, `e0`.`Description`, `e0`.`Difficulty`, `e0`.`LocationId`, `e0`.`MaxPlayers`, `e0`.`Name`, `e0`.`Price`, `l`.`Id` AS `Id0`, `l`.`Address`, `l`.`City`, `l`.`DeletedAt` AS `DeletedAt0`, `l`.`Latitude`, `l`.`Longitude`, `l`.`PostalCode`, `c`.`Id` AS `Id1`, `c`.`DeletedAt` AS `DeletedAt1`, `c`.`Name` AS `Name0`, `c`.`Website`, `e`.`EscapeRoomsId`, `e`.`ThemesId`, `r0`.`Id` AS `Id2`, `r0`.`Comment`, `r0`.`CreatedAt` AS `CreatedAt0`, `r0`.`DeletedAt` AS `DeletedAt2`, `r0`.`EscapeRoomId`, `r0`.`IsVerified`, `r0`.`PlayersCount`, `r0`.`Rating`, `r0`.`UserId`, `r0`.`VisitedAt`
    FROM `EscapeRoomTheme` AS `e`
    INNER JOIN `EscapeRooms` AS `e0` ON `e`.`EscapeRoomsId` = `e0`.`Id`
    INNER JOIN `Locations` AS `l` ON `e0`.`LocationId` = `l`.`Id`
    INNER JOIN `Companies` AS `c` ON `e0`.`CompanyId` = `c`.`Id`
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT `r`.`Id`, `r`.`Comment`, `r`.`CreatedAt`, `r`.`DeletedAt`, `r`.`EscapeRoomId`, `r`.`IsVerified`, `r`.`PlayersCount`, `r`.`Rating`, `r`.`UserId`, `r`.`VisitedAt`
        FROM `Reviews` AS `r`
        WHERE `r`.`DeletedAt` IS NULL
    ) AS `r0` ON `e0`.`Id` = `r0`.`EscapeRoomId`
    WHERE `e0`.`DeletedAt` IS NULL
) AS `s` ON `t`.`Id` = `s`.`ThemesId`
WHERE `t`.`DeletedAt` IS NULL
ORDER BY `t`.`Id`, `s`.`EscapeRoomsId`, `s`.`ThemesId`, `s`.`Id`, `s`.`Id0`, `s`.`Id1`
